LoadingScreen/Help01=您可以通过按下<k val="ControlGroupAssign1"/>键对单位进行编组。按下<k val="ControlGroupRecall1"/>键便可以重新选中编组中的单位。 /// You can store a unit selection by pressing<k val="ControlGroupAssign1"/>. Press<k val="ControlGroupRecall1"/> to recall the selection.
LoadingScreen/Help02=按下<k val="SubgroupNext"/>键可以在选中的单位中切换兵种，使单位技能的使用更为简单。 /// Press<k val="SubgroupNext"/> to cycle through different types of selected units, making it easier to use their abilities.
LoadingScreen/Help03=位于高地上的单位在作战时不会遭到还击。命令单位移上斜坡或调遣空中单位都可以帮助您获得视野，对付高地上的敌人。 /// Units on higher ground can attack without endangering themselves. To counter this, gain vision of the attackers by running up ramps or bringing air units.
LoadingScreen/Help04=萨尔纳加瞭望塔能够提供开阔的视野。将单位移至瞭望塔附近可将其激活。 /// Xel'Naga Towers provide vision across a large area. Stand a unit near a Xel'Naga Tower to control it.
LoadingScreen/Help05=摧毁岩石可打通前往新区域的通道。 /// Rocks can be destroyed to open up new paths.
LoadingScreen/Help06=起始区域的资源将迟早会消耗殆尽。向其它资源点扩张以保证稳定的收入。 /// Your starting area will eventually run out of resources. Expand to new resource locations to secure additional income.
LoadingScreen/Help07=早期建立分基地进行扩张是一种冒险的举动，但额外的资源收入有时值得您去这样做。 /// Expanding to a new resource location early in a game is risky, but the extra income is sometimes worth the risk.
LoadingScreen/Help08=武器和护甲升级会对现有及随后生产的单位产生影响，因此战斗持续越久，升级带来的受益便越多。 /// Weapon and armor upgrades affect existing and future units, so their benefits quickly add up over the course of longer games.
LoadingScreen/Help09=持续生产SCV、探机或工蜂是推动经济发展的关键。 /// The key to a strong economy is constantly training SCVs, Probes, or Drones.

LoadingScreen/Help11=利用编组功能，您在镜头不切换至基地的情况下便可以生产单位。 /// You can use control groups to train units without even looking at your base.

LoadingScreen/Help13=高产矿脉晶体矿的颜色为黄色，对其进行采集的效率高于普通晶体矿脉。 /// Rich Mineral Fields are yellow, and can be harvested faster than normal Mineral Fields.
LoadingScreen/Help14=摧毁所有敌人的建筑或最后一个离开游戏，才能获得一场多人游戏的胜利。 /// To win a multiplayer game, destroy all enemy structures or be the last player still in the game.

LoadingScreen/Help16=武器描述中的“vs 重甲：5”表示该武器对重甲目标造成的伤害为5点。 /// Weapons that list damage as "vs Armored: 5" do a total of 5 damage to targets that are considered Armored.
LoadingScreen/Help17=敌人在不借助侦测单位帮助的情况下无法攻击隐形或潜地的单位，铁鸦、侦测器或眼虫都属于侦测单位。 /// Cloaked or burrowed units cannot be attacked unless spotted by a detector, such as a Raven, Observer, or Overseer.

LoadingScreen/Help22=在战斗中，使用一些SCV对关键性防御设施或作战单位进行修理以协助战斗。 /// Use several SCVs to keep vital defenses or combat units alive during a fight.
LoadingScreen/Help23=使用医疗运输机配合大型步兵作战团队的战斗。利用其运输能力将步兵单位运送至敌后，展开奇袭。 /// Use Medivacs to support large infantry groups. Use their transport abilities to take infantry behind enemy lines for surprise attacks.
LoadingScreen/Help24=恶火的火焰喷射器可对火力线覆盖的所有敌方单位造成伤害。靠近大批聚集的敌人后发动攻击，以使造成的伤害最大化。 /// Hellions do damage in a straight line with their flame thrower. Get close to packs of enemies to maximize your damage.

Skin/Info/BanelingMecha=重造爆虫对工程师们提出了一项特殊的难题，因为他们千辛万苦采集到的酸液囊会不断溶解周遭一切钢化结构。幸运的是，他们最终成功了。 /// The recreation of the baneling posed a unique problem for engineers, as their carefully harvested acid sacs kept melting through the surrounding plate infrastructure. Eventually, they made it work.
Skin/Info/BanelingNest=异虫的巢群里必须要有一个爆虫巢穴来提供爆虫的基因代码。一旦筑巢完毕，战场上的任意一只跳虫就可以被命令在短时间内形成一个肉质的虫蛹，接着它们会以爆虫的形态破壳而出——变异成一种肮脏、臃肿的生物，其背部不停颤动着一团球状的、充满强酸的绿色囊泡。 /// The zerg hive cluster must have a baneling nest to add the baneling breed's genetic code. Once a nest is in place, any zergling on the field can be commanded to form a fleshy chrysalis for a brief pupation state, and then it will burst forth as a baneling--a foul, bloated creature with bulbous, acid-filled green sacs pulsating on its back.

Skin/Info/WarpPrismGolden=古代圣堂武士折跃棱镜具有一种非常特别的水晶晶格，其特殊之处就在于它有时候甚至能反射出其所运载的战士的神经图案。 /// Ancient Templar warp prisms featured a distinctive crystal lattice that would sometimes reflect the neural patterns of the warriors they transport.
Skin/Info/WarpPrismIhanrii=展开的伊罕利折跃棱镜会唤起星灵们对一种花的回忆，这种花曾经长满了他们家乡的山坡，只是那里已经换了一个新的名字——泰拉多尔九号星。 /// Unfurled, the Ihan-rii warp prism evokes a flower that once covered the hillsides of their homeworld, referred to by its current residents as "Tyrador IX."  
Skin/Info/WarpPrismNerazim=达拉姆相位技师有了新突破，现在折跃棱镜可以使用虚空能量了。这些变种被称为相位棱镜，已经在奈拉齐姆指挥官中获得了极高的人气。 /// Daelaam phase-smiths have broken new ground by adapting warp prisms to use Void energy. These variants, known as phase prisms, have already earned great popularity with Nerazim commanders.
Skin/Info/WarpPrismPurifier=如果有必要的话，净化者的折跃棱镜可以将一个智能人格在不同的机体之间进行自动传输，而折跃棱镜可以让这一切发生在战场上的各地。 /// Purifier warp prisms can automatically transfer an AI personality between different shells if needed, and warp prisms enable this to happen anywhere on the battlefield. 
Skin/Info/WarpPrismTaldarim=是否给折跃棱镜装备高级武器一直是舰队领主之间争论的焦点。对于其中一部分人而言，能够直接向战场输送部队就已足以。 /// Arming warp prisms with advanced weaponry is a point of contention among the fleet lords. Some prefer to use them to simply deploy their own warriors onto the battlefield.
Skin/Info/WidowMine=最初由维克多·卡琴斯基发明的寡妇雷，现已被优化成极其致命的军事设备。它可以对任何可疑的目标发射防御性飞弹。 /// Initially developed by Victor Kachinsky, the widow mine has been refined into a surprisingly lethal device that can fire defensive missiles against unsuspecting enemies.
Skin/Info/WidowMineCovertOps=饱受走火事故困扰的技术人员决定给寡妇雷增加防护性更好的板甲，以便能防止事故发生，减少意外伤亡。 /// Perplexed by occasional misfires in the past, technicians have added more protective plating to the widow mines to better contain accidents and protect against unintended injuries.
Skin/Info/WidowMineJunker=经过若干轮的超强破坏力实验后，米拉的雇佣兵们重新设计了他们的寡妇雷，以便能装纳额外的武器和炸药。 /// After several rounds of heavily destructive experimentation, Mira's mercs redesigned their widow mines to accommodate additional weaponry and explosives.
Skin/Info/WidowMineSilver=尽管不时就有各种血淋淋的事故成为新闻，但在泰拉多尔九号星的上流社会里，光滑闪亮的寡妇雷仍然被许多人当做宠物。 /// Despite gory accidents that make the news from time to time, sleek and shiny widow mines remain a common pet in the upper-class households of Tyrador IX.
Skin/Info/WidowMineUmojan=一直钟情于机器人技术的尤摩扬工程师们举行了一场特殊比赛，以图造出最完美的寡妇雷机器人。然而令他们震惊的是，最终的优胜者竟然是一位尚未完成学业的女学生。 /// Always fond of robotics, the Umojan engineers held an exclusive competition to craft the perfect widow mine and were thrilled to discover that the winner was still a student finishing her degree.
Skin/Info/Zealot=狂热者在战场上是一群无可匹敌的战士，他们经受数十年的刻苦训练，只为完善自己的各种战斗技巧。其标志性的灵能之刃是用他们自身的灵能能量形成的。 /// Peerless warriors on the battlefield, zealots undergo decades of intense training in order to perfect their combat skills. Their signature psi-blades are formed with their own psionic energy.
Skin/Info/ZealotGolden=许多狂热者很快就跟随了高阶圣堂武士的脚步，开始纪念星灵黄金时代的一切，包括那个时代的艺术与文化成就。然而，这场运动至今尚未获得官方认可。 /// Many zealots were quick to follow the high templar in celebrating the protoss' golden age, along with its artistic and cultural achievements. However, the movement has received no official recognition thus far.
Skin/Info/ZealotIhanrii=伊罕利星灵的狂热者们相信，萨尔那加终有一天会再度归来，给所有英勇的战士赐予永恒的神性。 /// Zealots of the Ihan-rii protoss believe the xel'naga will return one day to bless valiant warriors with eternal godhood.
Skin/Info/ZealotPurifier=虽然警戒者们没有独立的人格，但是它们全都被编程为与其狂热者同胞们一样的高贵战士。 /// Though they do not possess unique personalities, the sentinels are programmed to be noble warriors equal to their zealot brethren.
Skin/Info/ZealotRemastered=为了展现他们的无畏精神， 许多狂热者在全面战争期间不戴头盔就奔赴战场。这种做法自那以后就被禁止了。 /// To demonstrate their fearlessness, many zealots went without head armor during the Great War. This practice has since been discontinued.
Skin/Info/ZealotTaldarim=在塔达林的升格之链中，地位最低的往往是最渴望证明自己的。塔达林的狂热者绝不是一位可以小觑的对手。 /// The lowest ranking links in the Chain of Ascension are also the ones most eager to prove themselves. A zealot of the Tal'darim is a dangerous foe to face.
Skin/Info/ZealotXPR=虽然最高议会不存在了，但是曾为其军事领导人效命的执政官们仍然忠诚于达拉姆。只要星灵存在一日，他们就会义无反顾地战斗到底。 /// Though the Conclave no longer exists, the praetors who served as its military leaders are still loyal to the Daelaam. For as long as the protoss live, they will continue to fight with valor.
Skin/Info/Zergling=跳虫极为凶猛狂暴，尤其是在被更高级的异虫生物指挥，成群结队地发起攻击时是最危险的。 /// Savage and feral, zerglings are most dangerous when attacking in large groups that are controlled by a larger and more advanced strain of zerg.
Skin/Info/ZerglingMecha=尽管外形和动作与真正的跳虫别无二致，但是这些仿生异虫是纯机械复制品，完全依靠电力能源运行，而非吸收敌人的DNA。 /// Though they look and act just like zerglings, the simulants are purely mechanical reproductions that run wholly on electrical power sources, rather than absorbing the DNA of their enemies.
Skin/Info/ZerglingPrimal=一些体型较小的原始跳虫一直以来都被认为和它们在虫群中的同行们别无二致，甚至它们的攻击能力都大同小异。 /// Some of the smaller primal zerglings have been known to resemble their counterparts in the Swarm, even to the point where they possess similar attack capabilities.
Skin/Info/ZerglingRCZ=跳虫的神经系统是如此的高度亢奋，塞伯鲁斯工程师们不得不加装两根新的触角天线才能控制它们正常移动。 /// Zergling nervous systems are so hyperactive that Cerberus engineers had to affix two antennas to control their movement properly.
Skin/Info/ZerglingWebby=跳虫的基因组缺失产生了不可预知的后果。目前在利维坦跳虫身上的生长并不是有意进化，而是它们极度简化的DNA所带来的副作用。 /// The reduction of the zergling genome has had unpredictable results. The growths present on Leviathan zerglings are not intentionally evolved, but a byproduct of their extremely simplified DNA.
Skin/Info/ZerglingXPR=很少有哪种异虫会比跳虫的生命周期更短。出现任何有可能延续生命的变异现象，都是值得观察和分析的。 /// Few zerg have a shorter life expectancy than the zergling. Any mutation that appears to increase that life expectancy is considered worthy of observation and analysis.
